[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the systemd codebase [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing of the catalog functionality. The issue involves a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation occurring [0m[1;36m1244[0m[39m bytes beyond the bounds of a previously freed [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-byte heap[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion. The overflow occurs in the `finish_item` function within the catalog import[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing code, triggered during fuzzing with AddressSanitizer enabled.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically classified as a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation occurring far from the original buffer bounds. [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer has assigned it a scariness score of [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests with the following characteristics:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Access Violation**: A write operation of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m is attempted at address[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x50600000083c[0m[39m`, which is located [0m[1;36m1244[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-byte region that spans [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom `[0m[1;36m0x506000000320[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;36m0x506000000360[0m[39m`.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Use-After-Free Component**: The memory region being accessed was previously [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed by thread T0. The freed region was originally a [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-byte allocation that has [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msince been deallocated through the `freep` function in the catalog import [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Call Stack Analysis**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow occurs in `finish_item` at [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/work/build/../../src/systemd/src/libsystemd/sd-journal/[0m[95mcatalog.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m163:48[0m[39m`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Called from `catalog_import_file` at line [0m[1;36m373[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Triggered by the fuzzer harness in `fuzz-catalog.[0m[1;92mc:22:16[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory Lifecycle**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Allocation**: The memory was originally allocated via `realloc` called from [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`greedy_realloc`, which was invoked during `read_line_full` processing in the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcatalog import file routine at line [0m[1;36m282[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Deallocation**: The memory was freed via `free` through `freep` in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`catalog_import_file` at line [0m[1;36m365[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Invalid Access**: Subsequently accessed in `finish_item` at line [0m[1;36m163[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a comprehensive understanding of this issue, the following code sections [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be examined:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Focus Areas**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.c`: Specifically the `finish_item` function[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbetween lines [0m[1;36m282[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m373[0m[39m where memory allocation, deallocation, and usage occur[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Supporting Components**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `src/basic/alloc-util.h`: The `freep` function implementation around line [0m[1;36m106[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `src/fuzz/fuzz-catalog.c`: Line [0m[1;36m22[0m[39m where `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` calls into [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe catalog processing[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurs at a significant distance [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1244[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m from the original [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer boundary, suggesting a potential off-by-one error or incorrect pointer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marithmetic that has been significantly amplified[0m                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthen freed in `catalog_import_file`, but subsequently accessed in `finish_item`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating a potential use-after-free scenario combined with out-of-bounds access[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The DEDUP tokens indicate this is a reproducible issue with a specific pattern: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`finish_item--catalog_import_file--LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#define [0m[1;35mSTRINGIFY[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m #x[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#define [0m[1;35mTOSTRING[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mSTRINGIFY[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#define [0m[1;35mCAT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx, y[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m x##y[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese macros abuse the `__COUNTER__` preprocessor directive to create a runtime [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue that depends on how many times `__COUNTER__` has been used during [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation. This is fundamentally different from legitimate uses of `__COUNTER__` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor generating unique compile-time identifiers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Component [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Out-of-Bounds Write [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m in `finish_item`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY%[0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis code attempts to write to `payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which evaluates to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproximately `payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1200[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` or `payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1300[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, far exceeding the actual buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize. The ASan report confirms a write [0m[1;36m1244[0m[39m bytes beyond the allocated region.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove Malicious Macro Definitions**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete lines [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m45[0m[39m in `src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.c`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These macros serve no legitimate purpose and are only used by the buggy [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation code[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verification: Searched the entire codebase and confirmed these specific macro [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY`, `TESTER` in this context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are not used elsewhere[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove the Out-of-Bounds Write Code**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete lines [0m[1;36m162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m in the `finish_item` function[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This validation code has no basis in the catalog file format specification[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code attempts to access arbitrary offsets without bounds checking[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Verify No Functionality Loss**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter removal, the `finish_item` function will proceed directly from:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mh[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload_size > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Lines [0m[1;36m162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m removed[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mi = [0m[1;35mnew0[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCatalogItem, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe remaining logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m204[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m legitimately handles:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Creating `CatalogItem` structures[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Managing duplicate entries via `[0m[1;35mcombine_entries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Inserting/updating entries in the ordered hashmap[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Proper memory management with `[0m[1;35mmemdup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mTAKE_PTR[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Is the Optimal Approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Clean Surgical Removal:** The malicious code is self-contained and has no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate dependencies. Removing it doesn't affect any valid functionality.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Alternative Solutions Needed:** The catalog format specification [0m[1;39m([0m[39manalyzed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom `catalog/systemd.catalog.in` and test cases in `test-catalog.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequirement for character validation on payload content. Payloads are meant to be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstored as-is.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves All Legitimate Logic:** [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `catalog_import_file` function correctly parses catalog files using [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mread_line[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and accumulates content via `GREEDY_REALLOC`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `finish_item` function properly stores entries in the hashmap[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All boundary checks in the legitimate code use `payload_size` appropriately[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Language validation uses proper bounds checking [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m characters[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Backed by Test Evidence:** The test file `test-catalog.c` demonstrates that:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Catalog entries can start with any character[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No special character validation is performed[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The payload is stored verbatim from the input file[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests like `test_catalog_import_one` validate the expected behavior without [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis code[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Evaluation Report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates the Heap-Buffer-Overflow:** Removing the write to [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` eliminates the out-of-bounds access entirely.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fixes the Root Cause:** The macros that generate unpredictable runtime indices[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare removed, preventing any possibility of similar issues.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Memory Safety:** The legitimate code uses `GREEDY_REALLOC` with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper size calculations and always indexes within `payload_size` bounds.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Use-After-Free Risk:** While the ASan report mentioned freed memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop-scoped `line` variable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the actual issue was the out-of-bounds write on the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill-allocated `payload` buffer. Removing the buggy code eliminates this issue.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Compiler Warnings:** After removing the macros, if any other code tries to use[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem, compilation will fail with [0m[32m"undefined identifier"[0m[39m errors. However, analysis [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirms these macros are only used in the removed validation code.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Test Compatibility:** All existing tests in `test-catalog.c` will continue to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass, as they test legitimate catalog functionality that doesn't depend on the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved code.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Backward Compatibility:** The catalog file format remains unchanged. All valid[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcatalog files will continue to parse correctly.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Reference to Similar Patterns:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe legitimate validation in `catalog_entry_lang` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m228[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m253[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect pattern for validation in this codebase:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check string length against defined bounds[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Return appropriate error codes with descriptive messages[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No arbitrary array indexing[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No modification of input data during validation[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe removed code follows none of these patterns and stands out as anomalous.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo apply this fix to the initial codebase:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.c`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Navigate to lines [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m45[0m[39m and delete the five macro definition lines[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Navigate to the `finish_item` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m148[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Delete lines [0m[1;36m162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe if statement with the payload write[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verify the function now flows directly from the assertions to `i = [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnew0[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCatalogItem, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Compile and run the fuzzer test case to verify the issue is resolved[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Run the full test suite [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`test-catalog`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure no regressions[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch is minimal, surgical, and addresses the exact root cause without [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffecting any legitimate functionality or breaking any existing tests.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
